## bob.core.DataGraph
- __add__(self, other: 'Graph') -> 'Graph'  —  Set-theoretic union BNode IDs are not changed.
- __and__(self, other: 'Graph') -> 'Graph'  —  Set-theoretic intersection. BNode IDs are not changed.
- __gt__(self, other) -> 'bool'  —  Return self>value.
- __iadd__(self: '_GraphT', other: 'Iterable[_TripleType]') -> '_GraphT'  —  Add all triples in Graph other to Graph. BNode IDs are not changed.
- __isub__(self: '_GraphT', other: 'Iterable[_TripleType]') -> '_GraphT'  —  Subtract all triples in Graph other from Graph. BNode IDs are not changed.
- __or__(self, other: 'Graph') -> 'Graph'  —  Set-theoretic union BNode IDs are not changed.
- __sub__(self, other: 'Graph') -> 'Graph'  —  Set-theoretic difference. BNode IDs are not changed.
- __xor__(self, other: 'Graph') -> 'Graph'  —  Set-theoretic XOR. BNode IDs are not changed.
